def items_fit_exactly_in_boxes(
    items: Annotated[list[Item], Len(8, 8)],
    assignments: Annotated[list[BoxAssignment], Len(8, 8)],
    box_width: int,
    box_height: int
):
    for i in range(1, N_ITEMS + 1):
        item : Item = items[i]
        assignment : BoxAssignment = assignments[i]

        assert assignment.y >= 0

# --- Auxiliary Variables ---
# Leave empty, if not required.
# --- constraints ---
def no_overlap(
    assignments: Annotated[list[BoxAssignment], Len(8, 8)],
    items: Annotated[list[Item], Len(8, 8)]
):
    for i in range(1, N_ITEMS + 1):
        for j in range(i + 1, N_ITEMS + 1):
            assignment_i : BoxAssignment = assignments[i]
            assignment_j : BoxAssignment = assignments[j]
            item_i : Item = items[i]
            item_j : Item = items[j]

```python
from typing import Annotated
from pydantic import Field

# --- Objects ---
Item = DSRecord({
    "width": Annotated[int, Field(strict=True, ge=1, le=5)],
    "height": Annotated[int, Field(strict=True, ge=1, le=9)]
})

BoxAssignment = DSRecord({
    "box_id": Annotated[int, Field(strict=True, ge=1, le=8)],
    "x": Annotated[int, Field(strict=True, ge=0, le=5)],
    "y": Annotated[int, Field(strict=True, ge=0, le=12)]
})
```



# --- Constants ---
BOX_HEIGHT : int = 12
BOX_WIDTH : int = 5
ITEM1 : Item = {"width": 3, "height": 4}
ITEM2 : Item = {"width": 1, "height": 2}
ITEM3 : Item = {"width": 5, "height": 4}
ITEM4 : Item = {"width": 2, "height": 4}
ITEM5 : Item = {"width": 1, "height": 3}
ITEM6 : Item = {"width": 5, "height": 9}
ITEM7 : Item = {"width": 5, "height": 3}
ITEM8 : Item = {"width": 5, "height": 1}
ITEMS : Annotated[list[Item], Len(8, 8)] = [ITEM1, ITEM2, ITEM3, ITEM4, ITEM5, ITEM6, ITEM7, ITEM8]
N_ITEMS : int = 8
nr_used_boxes : Annotated[int, Field(strict=True, ge=1, le=8)]
item_box_assignments : Annotated[list[BoxAssignment], Len(8, 8)]
x_y_positions : Annotated[list[BoxAssignment], Len(8, 8)]


# -- Objective --


objective = nr_used_boxes

# --- objective ---
def calculate_objective(assignments: Annotated[list[BoxAssignment], Len(8, 8)]) -> int:
    max_box_id = 0
    for i in range(1, N_ITEMS + 1):
        box_id = assignments[i].box_id
        if box_id > max_box_id:
            max_box_id = box_id
    return max_box_id

calculated_objective_value = calculate_objective(item_box_assignments)
objective = calculated_objective_value

# -- Constraints --


# --- Auxiliary Variables ---
# Leave empty, if not required.
# --- constraints ---
def items_fit_exactly_in_boxes(
    items: Annotated[list[Item], Len(8, 8)],
    assignments: Annotated[list[BoxAssignment], Len(8, 8)],
    box_width: int,
    box_height: int
):
    for i in range(1, N_ITEMS + 1):
        item : Item = items[i]
        assignment : BoxAssignment = assignments[i]
        x_end : int = assignment.x + item.width
        y_end : int = assignment.y + item.height
        assert assignment.x >= 0
        assert assignment.y >= 0
        assert x_end <= box_width
        assert y_end <= box_height

items_fit_exactly_in_boxes(ITEMS, item_box_assignments, BOX_WIDTH, BOX_HEIGHT)

# --- Auxiliary Variables ---
# Leave empty, if not required.
# --- constraints ---
def no_overlap(
    assignments: Annotated[list[BoxAssignment], Len(8, 8)],
    items: Annotated[list[Item], Len(8, 8)]
):
    for i in range(1, N_ITEMS + 1):
        for j in range(i + 1, N_ITEMS + 1):
            assignment_i : BoxAssignment = assignments[i]
            assignment_j : BoxAssignment = assignments[j]
            item_i : Item = items[i]
            item_j : Item = items[j]

            # Calculate boundaries for item i
            x1_i : int = assignment_i.x
            x2_i : int = assignment_i.x + item_i.width
            y1_i : int = assignment_i.y
            y2_i : int = assignment_i.y + item_i.height

            # Calculate boundaries for item j
            x1_j : int = assignment_j.x
            x2_j : int = assignment_j.x + item_j.width
            y1_j : int = assignment_j.y
            y2_j : int = assignment_j.y + item_j.height

            # Check if boxes are different
            boxes_different : bool = assignment_i.box_id != assignment_j.box_id

            # Check for overlap in the same box
            horizontal_overlap : bool = not (x2_i <= x1_j or x2_j <= x1_i)
            vertical_overlap : bool = not (y2_i <= y1_j or y2_j <= y1_i)
            same_box : bool = assignment_i.box_id == assignment_j.box_id
            overlap : bool = horizontal_overlap and vertical_overlap and same_box

            assert boxes_different or not overlap

no_overlap(item_box_assignments, ITEMS)

def fit_items_in_boxes(
    items: Annotated[list[Item], Len(8, 8)],
    positions: Annotated[list[Position], Len(8, 8)],
    assignments: Annotated[list[int], Len(8, 8)],
    box_width: int,
    box_height: int
):
    for i in range(1, N_ITEMS + 1):
        item : Item = items[i]
        pos : Position = positions[i]
        box_id : int = assignments[i]

        # Ensure the item fits within the box dimensions
        assert pos.x + item.width <= box_width
        assert pos.y + item.height <= box_height

        # Ensure the item is placed within the valid coordinate range
        assert pos.x >= 0
        assert pos.y >= 0

# --- Auxiliary Variables ---
# Leave empty, if not required.
# --- constraints ---
def no_overlap(
    items: Annotated[list[Item], Len(8, 8)],
    positions: Annotated[list[Position], Len(8, 8)],
    assignments: Annotated[list[int], Len(8, 8)]
):
    for i in range(1, N_ITEMS + 1):
        for j in range(i + 1, N_ITEMS + 1):
            # Only check for overlap if both items are in the same box
            if assignments[i] == assignments[j]:
                pos_i : Position = positions[i]
                pos_j : Position = positions[j]
                item_i : Item = items[i]
                item_j : Item = items[j]

                # Check for non-overlapping conditions
                assert pos_i.x + item_i.width <= pos_j.x or \
                       pos_j.x + item_j.width <= pos_i.x or \
                       pos_i.y + item_i.height <= pos_j.y or \
                       pos_j.y + item_j.height <= pos_i.y

# --- objective ---
def calculate_objective(assignments: Annotated[list[int], Len(8, 8)]) -> int:
    max_box = 0
    for i in range(1, N_ITEMS + 1):
        if assignments[i] > max_box:
            max_box = assignments[i]
    return max_box

calculated_objective_value = calculate_objective(item_box_assignments)
objective = calculated_objective_value

# -- Constraints --


# --- Auxiliary Variables ---
# Leave empty, if not required.
# --- constraints ---
def fit_items_in_boxes(
    items: Annotated[list[Item], Len(8, 8)],
    positions: Annotated[list[Position], Len(8, 8)],
    assignments: Annotated[list[int], Len(8, 8)],
    box_width: int,
    box_height: int
):
    for i in range(1, N_ITEMS + 1):
        item : Item = items[i]
        pos : Position = positions[i]
        box_id : int = assignments[i]

        # Ensure the item fits within the box dimensions
        assert pos.x + item.width <= box_width
        assert pos.y + item.height <= box_height

        # Ensure the item is placed within the valid coordinate range
        assert pos.x >= 0
        assert pos.y >= 0

fit_items_in_boxes(ITEMS, x_y_positions, item_box_assignments, BOX_WIDTH, BOX_HEIGHT)

# --- Auxiliary Variables ---
# Leave empty, if not required.
# --- constraints ---
def no_overlap(
    items: Annotated[list[Item], Len(8, 8)],
    positions: Annotated[list[Position], Len(8, 8)],
    assignments: Annotated[list[int], Len(8, 8)]
):
    for i in range(1, N_ITEMS + 1):
        for j in range(i + 1, N_ITEMS + 1):
            # Only check for overlap if both items are in the same box
            if assignments[i] == assignments[j]:
                pos_i : Position = positions[i]
                pos_j : Position = positions[j]
                item_i : Item = items[i]
                item_j : Item = items[j]

                # Check for non-overlapping conditions
                assert pos_i.x + item_i.width <= pos_j.x or \
                       pos_j.x + item_j.width <= pos_i.x or \
                       pos_i.y + item_i.height <= pos_j.y or \
                       pos_j.y + item_j.height <= pos_i.y

no_overlap(ITEMS, x_y_positions, item_box_assignments)

# --- constraints ---
def ensure_item_in_one_box(
    assignments: Annotated[list[int], Len(8, 8)]
):
    for i in range(1, N_ITEMS + 1):
        assert assignments[i] >= 1
        assert assignments[i] <= 8

# --- constraints ---
def no_overlap(
    assignments: Annotated[list[BoxAssignment], Len(8, 8)],
    items: Annotated[list[Item], Len(8, 8)]
) -> None:
    for i in range(1, N_ITEMS + 1):
        for j in range(i + 1, N_ITEMS + 1):
            # Only check overlap if both items are in the same box
            assert not (
                assignments[i].box_id == assignments[j].box_id and not (
                    assignments[i].x + items[i].width <= assignments[j].x or  # item1 is left of item2

                    assignments[j].y + items[j].height <= assignments[i].y     # item2 is below item1

objective = nr_used_boxes

# --- objective ---
def calculate_objective(assignments: Annotated[list[BoxAssignment], Len(8, 8)]) -> int:
    max_box_id = 0
    for i in range(1, N_ITEMS + 1):
        box_id = assignments[i].box_id
        if box_id > max_box_id:
            max_box_id = box_id
    return max_box_id

calculated_objective_value = calculate_objective(item_box_assignments)
objective = calculated_objective_value

# --- Auxiliary Variables ---
# Leave empty, if not required.
# --- constraints ---
def fit_items_in_boxes(
    items: Annotated[list[Item], Len(8, 8)],
    assignments: Annotated[list[BoxAssignment], Len(8, 8)]
) -> None:
    for i in range(1, N_ITEMS + 1):
        item_width = items[i].width
        item_height = items[i].height
        x_pos = assignments[i].x
        y_pos = assignments[i].y

        assert x_pos + item_width <= BOX_WIDTH
        assert y_pos + item_height <= BOX_HEIGHT

fit_items_in_boxes(ITEMS, item_box_assignments)

def items_fit_exactly_in_boxes(

    assignments: Annotated[list[BoxAssignment], Len(8, 8)],
    box_width: int,
    box_height: int
):
    # For each box, track total occupied area
    box_areas: Annotated[list[Annotated[int, Field(strict=True, ge=0, le=60)]], Len(8, 8)] = [0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0]

        assignment: BoxAssignment = assignments[i]
        box_id: int = assignment.box_id

        # Ensure item fits within box dimensions

        assert pos.y + item.height <= box_height

def pack_items_in_boxes(
    items: Annotated[list[Item], Len(8, 8)],
    assignments: Annotated[list[BoxAssignment], Len(8, 8)],
    positions: Annotated[list[Position], Len(8, 8)]
) -> None:

        assignment : BoxAssignment = assignments[i]
        position : Position = positions[i]

        assert item.height <= BOX_HEIGHT

        assert position.y + item.height <= BOX_HEIGHT

# --- Auxiliary Variables ---
# None needed
# --- constraints ---
def check_no_overlap(
    items: Annotated[list[Item], Len(8, 8)],
    assignments: Annotated[list[BoxAssignment], Len(8, 8)],
    positions: Annotated[list[Position], Len(8, 8)]
) -> None:
    for i in range(1, 9):
        for j in range(i + 1, 9):
            item_i : Item = items[i]
            item_j : Item = items[j]
            assignment_i : BoxAssignment = assignments[i]
            assignment_j : BoxAssignment = assignments[j]
            position_i : Position = positions[i]
            position_j : Position = positions[j]

            # Items must be in the same box to potentially overlap
            assert assignment_i.box_id != assignment_j.box_id or \
                   (position_i.x + item_i.width <= position_j.x or
                    position_j.x + item_j.width <= position_i.x or
                    position_i.y + item_i.height <= position_j.y or
                    position_j.y + item_j.height <= position_i.y)

check_no_overlap(ITEMS, item_box_assignments, x_y_positions)

def ensure_single_box_assignment(
    assignments: Annotated[list[BoxAssignment], Len(8, 8)]
) -> None:
    # Each item must be assigned to exactly one box
    for i in range(1, 9):
        assignment : BoxAssignment = assignments[i]
        assert assignment.box_id >= 1
        assert assignment.box_id <= 8

ensure_single_box_assignment(item_box_assignments)

def validate_placement_bounds(
    items: Annotated[list[Item], Len(8, 8)],
    assignments: Annotated[list[BoxAssignment], Len(8, 8)],
    positions: Annotated[list[Position], Len(8, 8)]
) -> None:
    # Validate that each item fits in its assigned box and doesn't exceed boundaries
    for i in range(1, 9):
        item : Item = items[i]
        assignment : BoxAssignment = assignments[i]
        position : Position = positions[i]

        # Box ID validity
        assert assignment.box_id >= 1
        assert assignment.box_id <= 8

        # Position validity
        assert position.x >= 0
        assert position.x <= 5
        assert position.y >= 0
        assert position.y <= 12

        # Item fits within box
        assert item.width <= BOX_WIDTH
        assert item.height <= BOX_HEIGHT

        # Placement within box boundaries
        assert position.x + item.width <= BOX_WIDTH
        assert position.y + item.height <= BOX_HEIGHT

validate_placement_bounds(ITEMS, item_box_assignments, x_y_positions)

def prevent_overlapping_items(
    items: Annotated[list[Item], Len(8, 8)],
    assignments: Annotated[list[BoxAssignment], Len(8, 8)],
    positions: Annotated[list[Position], Len(8, 8)]
) -> None:
    # Ensure no two items overlap in the same box
    for i in range(1, 9):
        for j in range(i + 1, 9):
            item_i : Item = items[i]
            item_j : Item = items[j]
            assignment_i : BoxAssignment = assignments[i]
            assignment_j : BoxAssignment = assignments[j]
            position_i : Position = positions[i]
            position_j : Position = positions[j]

            # Only check overlap if items are in the same box
            assert assignment_i.box_id != assignment_j.box_id or \
                   (position_i.x + item_i.width <= position_j.x or
                    position_j.x + item_j.width <= position_i.x or
                    position_i.y + item_i.height <= position_j.y or
                    position_j.y + item_j.height <= position_i.y)

prevent_overlapping_items(ITEMS, item_box_assignments, x_y_positions)

```python
from typing import Annotated
from pydantic import Field

# --- Objects ---
Item = DSRecord({
    "width": Annotated[int, Field(strict=True, ge=1, le=5)],
    "height": Annotated[int, Field(strict=True, ge=1, le=9)]
})

Position = DSRecord({
    "x": Annotated[int, Field(strict=True, ge=0, le=5)],
    "y": Annotated[int, Field(strict=True, ge=0, le=12)]
})

BoxAssignment = DSRecord({
    "box_id": Annotated[int, Field(strict=True, ge=1, le=8)],
    "position": Position
})
```

objective = nr_used_boxes

# --- objective ---
def calculate_objective(assignments: Annotated[list[BoxAssignment], Len(8, 8)]) -> int:
    max_box_id = 0
    for i in range(1, 9):
        box_id = assignments[i].box_id
        if box_id > max_box_id:
            max_box_id = box_id
    return max_box_id

calculated_objective_value = calculate_objective(item_box_assignments)
objective = calculated_objective_value

def pack_items_in_boxes(
    items: Annotated[list[Item], Len(8, 8)],
    assignments: Annotated[list[BoxAssignment], Len(8, 8)],
    positions: Annotated[list[Position], Len(8, 8)]
) -> None:
    for i in range(1, 9):
        item : Item = items[i]
        assignment : BoxAssignment = assignments[i]
        position : Position = positions[i]

        # Check that box_id is valid
        assert assignment.box_id >= 1
        assert assignment.box_id <= 8

        # Check that position coordinates are valid
        assert position.x >= 0
        assert position.x <= 5
        assert position.y >= 0
        assert position.y <= 12

        # Check that item fits within box dimensions
        assert item.width <= BOX_WIDTH
        assert item.height <= BOX_HEIGHT

        # Check that item placement does not exceed box boundaries
        assert position.x + item.width <= BOX_WIDTH
        assert position.y + item.height <= BOX_HEIGHT

            position_i : Position = positions[i]
            position_j : Position = positions[j]

                   (position_i.x + item_i.width <= position_j.x or
                    position_j.x + item_j.width <= position_i.x or

def fit_items_in_boxes(
    items: Annotated[list[Item], Len(8, 8)],
    assignments: Annotated[list[BoxAssignment], Len(8, 8)],
    box_width: int,
    box_height: int
):
    for i in range(1, N_ITEMS + 1):
        item: Item = items[i]
        pos: Position = assignments[i].position
        x_end: int = pos.x + item.width
        y_end: int = pos.y + item.height

        assert pos.y >= 0
        assert x_end <= box_width
        assert y_end <= box_height

# --- constraints ---
def no_overlap(
    items: Annotated[list[Item], Len(8, 8)],
    assignments: Annotated[list[BoxAssignment], Len(8, 8)]
):
    for i in range(1, N_ITEMS + 1):
        for j in range(i + 1, N_ITEMS + 1):
            if assignments[i].box_id == assignments[j].box_id:
                assert not (
                    assignments[i].position.x < assignments[j].position.x + items[j].width and
                    assignments[j].position.x < assignments[i].position.x + items[i].width and
                    assignments[i].position.y < assignments[j].position.y + items[j].height and
                    assignments[j].position.y < assignments[i].position.y + items[i].height
                )

no_overlap(ITEMS, item_box_assignments)

# -- Objects --


```python
from typing import Annotated
from pydantic import Field

# --- Objects ---
Item = DSRecord({
    "width": Annotated[int, Field(strict=True, ge=1, le=5)],
    "height": Annotated[int, Field(strict=True, ge=1, le=9)]
})

Position = DSRecord({
    "x": Annotated[int, Field(strict=True, ge=0, le=5)],
    "y": Annotated[int, Field(strict=True, ge=0, le=12)]
})

BoxAssignment = DSRecord({
    "box_id": Annotated[int, Field(strict=True, ge=1, le=8)],
    "position": Position
})
```



# --- Constants ---
BOX_HEIGHT : int = 12
BOX_WIDTH : int = 5
ITEM1 : Item = {"width": 3, "height": 4}
ITEM2 : Item = {"width": 1, "height": 2}
ITEM3 : Item = {"width": 5, "height": 4}
ITEM4 : Item = {"width": 2, "height": 4}
ITEM5 : Item = {"width": 1, "height": 3}
ITEM6 : Item = {"width": 5, "height": 9}
ITEM7 : Item = {"width": 5, "height": 3}
ITEM8 : Item = {"width": 5, "height": 1}
ITEMS : Annotated[list[Item], Len(8, 8)] = [ITEM1, ITEM2, ITEM3, ITEM4, ITEM5, ITEM6, ITEM7, ITEM8]
N_ITEMS : int = 8
nr_used_boxes : Annotated[int, Field(strict=True, ge=1, le=8)]
item_box_assignments : Annotated[list[BoxAssignment], Len(8, 8)]
x_y_positions : Annotated[list[Position], Len(8, 8)]


# -- Objective --


objective = nr_used_boxes

# --- objective ---
def calculate_objective(assignments: Annotated[list[BoxAssignment], Len(8, 8)]) -> int:
    max_box_id = 0
    for i in range(1, N_ITEMS + 1):
        box_id = assignments[i].box_id
        if box_id > max_box_id:
            max_box_id = box_id
    return max_box_id

calculated_objective_value = calculate_objective(item_box_assignments)
objective = calculated_objective_value

# -- Constraints --


# --- Auxiliary Variables ---
# Leave empty, if not required.
# --- constraints ---
def fit_items_in_boxes(
    items: Annotated[list[Item], Len(8, 8)],
    assignments: Annotated[list[BoxAssignment], Len(8, 8)],
    box_width: int,
    box_height: int
):
    for i in range(1, N_ITEMS + 1):
        item: Item = items[i]
        pos: Position = assignments[i].position
        x_end: int = pos.x + item.width
        y_end: int = pos.y + item.height
        assert pos.x >= 0
        assert pos.y >= 0
        assert x_end <= box_width
        assert y_end <= box_height

fit_items_in_boxes(ITEMS, item_box_assignments, BOX_WIDTH, BOX_HEIGHT)

# --- constraints ---
def no_overlap(
    items: Annotated[list[Item], Len(8, 8)],
    assignments: Annotated[list[BoxAssignment], Len(8, 8)]
):
    for i in range(1, N_ITEMS + 1):
        for j in range(i + 1, N_ITEMS + 1):
            if assignments[i].box_id == assignments[j].box_id:
                assert not (
                    assignments[i].position.x < assignments[j].position.x + items[j].width and
                    assignments[j].position.x < assignments[i].position.x + items[i].width and
                    assignments[i].position.y < assignments[j].position.y + items[j].height and
                    assignments[j].position.y < assignments[i].position.y + items[i].height
                )

no_overlap(ITEMS, item_box_assignments)

):

        box_id = assignments[i].box_id
        assert box_id >= 1
        assert box_id <= 8

# --- Auxiliary Variables ---
# Leave empty, if not required.
# --- constraints ---
def no_overlap(
    assignments: Annotated[list[BoxAssignment], Len(8, 8)],
    items: Annotated[list[Item], Len(8, 8)]
):
    for i in range(1, N_ITEMS + 1):
        for j in range(i + 1, N_ITEMS + 1):
            assignment_i : BoxAssignment = assignments[i]
            assignment_j : BoxAssignment = assignments[j]
            item_i : Item = items[i]
            item_j : Item = items[j]

            # Check if both items are in the same box
            if assignment_i.box_id == assignment_j.box_id:
                # Check for non-overlapping on x-axis
                x_overlap : bool = not (
                    assignment_i.x + item_i.width <= assignment_j.x or
                    assignment_j.x + item_j.width <= assignment_i.x
                )

                # Check for non-overlapping on y-axis
                y_overlap : bool = not (
                    assignment_i.y + item_i.height <= assignment_j.y or
                    assignment_j.y + item_j.height <= assignment_i.y
                )

                # If both overlap on x and y axis, then there is an overlap
                assert not (x_overlap and y_overlap)

no_overlap(item_box_assignments, ITEMS)

# --- constraints ---
def ensure_item_box_assignment_validity(
    assignments: Annotated[list[BoxAssignment], Len(8, 8)]
):
    for i in range(1, N_ITEMS + 1):
        assignment : BoxAssignment = assignments[i]
        assert assignment.box_id >= 1
        assert assignment.box_id <= 8
        assert assignment.x >= 0
        assert assignment.x <= 5
        assert assignment.y >= 0
        assert assignment.y <= 12

ensure_item_box_assignment_validity(item_box_assignments)

```python
# --- Objects ---
Item = DSRecord({
    "width": Annotated[int, Field(strict=True, ge=1, le=5)],
    "height": Annotated[int, Field(strict=True, ge=1, le=9)]
})

BoxAssignment = DSRecord({
    "box_id": Annotated[int, Field(strict=True, ge=1, le=8)],
    "x": Annotated[int, Field(strict=True, ge=0, le=5)],
    "y": Annotated[int, Field(strict=True, ge=0, le=12)]
})
```

# --- Constants ---
BOX_HEIGHT : int = 12
BOX_WIDTH : int = 5
ITEM1 : Item = {"width": 3, "height": 4}
ITEM2 : Item = {"width": 1, "height": 2}
ITEM3 : Item = {"width": 5, "height": 4}
ITEM4 : Item = {"width": 2, "height": 4}
ITEM5 : Item = {"width": 1, "height": 3}
ITEM6 : Item = {"width": 5, "height": 9}
ITEM7 : Item = {"width": 5, "height": 3}
ITEM8 : Item = {"width": 5, "height": 1}
ITEMS : Annotated[list[Item], Len(8, 8)] = [ITEM1, ITEM2, ITEM3, ITEM4, ITEM5, ITEM6, ITEM7, ITEM8]
N_ITEMS : int = 8
nr_used_boxes : Annotated[int, Field(strict=True, ge=1, le=8)]
item_box_assignments : Annotated[list[BoxAssignment], Len(8, 8)]
x_y_positions : Annotated[list[BoxAssignment], Len(8, 8)]


# -- Objective --


objective = nr_used_boxes

# --- objective ---
def calculate_objective(assignments: Annotated[list[BoxAssignment], Len(8, 8)]) -> int:
    max_box_id = 0
    for i in range(1, N_ITEMS + 1):
        box_id = assignments[i].box_id
        if box_id > max_box_id:
            max_box_id = box_id
    return max_box_id

calculated_objective_value = calculate_objective(item_box_assignments)
objective = calculated_objective_value

# -- Constraints --


# --- Auxiliary Variables ---
# Leave empty, if not required.
# --- constraints ---
def fit_items_in_boxes(
    items: Annotated[list[Item], Len(8, 8)],
    assignments: Annotated[list[BoxAssignment], Len(8, 8)],
    box_width: int,
    box_height: int
):
    for i in range(1, N_ITEMS + 1):
        item : Item = items[i]
        assignment : BoxAssignment = assignments[i]
        assert assignment.x + item.width <= box_width
        assert assignment.y + item.height <= box_height

fit_items_in_boxes(ITEMS, item_box_assignments, BOX_WIDTH, BOX_HEIGHT)

# --- Auxiliary Variables ---
# Leave empty, if not required.
# --- constraints ---
def no_overlap(
    assignments: Annotated[list[BoxAssignment], Len(8, 8)],
    items: Annotated[list[Item], Len(8, 8)]
):
    for i in range(1, N_ITEMS + 1):
        for j in range(i + 1, N_ITEMS + 1):
            assignment_i : BoxAssignment = assignments[i]
            assignment_j : BoxAssignment = assignments[j]
            item_i : Item = items[i]
            item_j : Item = items[j]

            # Check if both items are in the same box
            if assignment_i.box_id == assignment_j.box_id:
                # Check for non-overlapping on x-axis
                x_overlap : bool = not (
                    assignment_i.x + item_i.width <= assignment_j.x or
                    assignment_j.x + item_j.width <= assignment_i.x
                )

                # Check for non-overlapping on y-axis
                y_overlap : bool = not (
                    assignment_i.y + item_i.height <= assignment_j.y or
                    assignment_j.y + item_j.height <= assignment_i.y
                )

                # If both overlap on x and y axis, then there is an overlap
                assert not (x_overlap and y_overlap)

no_overlap(item_box_assignments, ITEMS)

# --- constraints ---
def ensure_item_box_assignment_validity(
    assignments: Annotated[list[BoxAssignment], Len(8, 8)]
):
    for i in range(1, N_ITEMS + 1):
        assignment : BoxAssignment = assignments[i]
        assert assignment.box_id >= 1
        assert assignment.box_id <= 8
        assert assignment.x >= 0
        assert assignment.x <= 5
        assert assignment.y >= 0
        assert assignment.y <= 12

ensure_item_box_assignment_validity(item_box_assignments)

def ensure_items_assigned_to_boxes(
    assignments: Annotated[list[BoxAssignment], Len(8, 8)]
):
    for i in range(1, N_ITEMS + 1):
        assignment : BoxAssignment = assignments[i]
        assert assignment.box_id >= 1
        assert assignment.box_id <= 8

ensure_items_assigned_to_boxes(item_box_assignments)

def fit_items_in_boxes(
    items: Annotated[list[Item], Len(8, 8)],
    assignments: Annotated[list[BoxAssignment], Len(8, 8)],
    box_width: int,
    box_height: int
):
    for i in range(1, N_ITEMS + 1):
        item : Item = items[i]
        assignment : BoxAssignment = assignments[i]
        assert assignment.x + item.width <= box_width
        assert assignment.y + item.height <= box_height

# --- constraints ---
def no_overlap(
    assignments: Annotated[list[BoxAssignment], Len(8, 8)],
    items: Annotated[list[Item], Len(8, 8)]
):
    for i in range(1, N_ITEMS + 1):
        for j in range(i + 1, N_ITEMS + 1):
            assignment_i : BoxAssignment = assignments[i]
            assignment_j : BoxAssignment = assignments[j]
            item_i : Item = items[i]
            item_j : Item = items[j]

            # Check for overlap only if in the same box
            assert (
                assignment_i.box_id != assignment_j.box_id or
                (assignment_i.x + item_i.width <= assignment_j.x or
                 assignment_j.x + item_j.width <= assignment_i.x or
                 assignment_i.y + item_i.height <= assignment_j.y or
                 assignment_j.y + item_j.height <= assignment_i.y)
            )

no_overlap(item_box_assignments, ITEMS)

objective = nr_used_boxes

# --- objective ---
def calculate_objective(assignments: Annotated[list[BoxAssignment], Len(8, 8)]) -> int:
    max_box_id = 0
    for i in range(1, N_ITEMS + 1):
        box_id = assignments[i].box_id
        if box_id > max_box_id:
            max_box_id = box_id
    return max_box_id

calculated_objective_value = calculate_objective(item_box_assignments)
objective = calculated_objective_value

# --- Auxiliary Variables ---
# Leave empty, if not required.
# --- constraints ---
def fit_items_in_boxes(
    items: Annotated[list[Item], Len(8, 8)],
    assignments: Annotated[list[BoxAssignment], Len(8, 8)],
    box_width: int,
    box_height: int
):
    for i in range(1, N_ITEMS + 1):
        item : Item = items[i]
        assignment : BoxAssignment = assignments[i]
        assert assignment.x + item.width <= box_width
        assert assignment.y + item.height <= box_height

fit_items_in_boxes(ITEMS, item_box_assignments, BOX_WIDTH, BOX_HEIGHT)

# --- constraints ---
def no_overlap(
    assignments: Annotated[list[BoxAssignment], Len(8, 8)],
    items: Annotated[list[Item], Len(8, 8)]
):
    for i in range(1, N_ITEMS + 1):
        for j in range(i + 1, N_ITEMS + 1):
            assignment_i : BoxAssignment = assignments[i]
            assignment_j : BoxAssignment = assignments[j]
            item_i : Item = items[i]
            item_j : Item = items[j]

            # Check for overlap only if in the same box
            assert (
                assignment_i.box_id != assignment_j.box_id or
                (assignment_i.x + item_i.width <= assignment_j.x or
                 assignment_j.x + item_j.width <= assignment_i.x or
                 assignment_i.y + item_i.height <= assignment_j.y or
                 assignment_j.y + item_j.height <= assignment_i.y)
            )

no_overlap(item_box_assignments, ITEMS)

# --- objective ---
def calculate_objective(assignments: Annotated[list[BoxAssignment], Len(8, 8)]) -> int:
    max_box_id = 0
    for i in range(1, N_ITEMS + 1):
        box_id = assignments[i].box_id
        if box_id > max_box_id:
            max_box_id = box_id
    return max_box_id

objective = calculated_objective_value

def items_fit_exactly_in_boxes(
    items: Annotated[list[Item], Len(8, 8)],
    assignments: Annotated[list[BoxAssignment], Len(8, 8)]

# --- constraints ---
def no_overlap_between_items(
    assignments: Annotated[list[BoxAssignment], Len(8, 8)],
    items: Annotated[list[Item], Len(8, 8)]
) -> None:
    for i in range(1, N_ITEMS + 1):
        for j in range(i + 1, N_ITEMS + 1):
            # Only check overlap if both items are in the same box
            assert (assignments[i].box_id != assignments[j].box_id) or \
                   (assignments[i].x + items[i].width <= assignments[j].x) or \
                   (assignments[j].x + items[j].width <= assignments[i].x) or \
                   (assignments[i].y + items[i].height <= assignments[j].y) or \
                   (assignments[j].y + items[j].height <= assignments[i].y)

# --- objective ---
def calculate_objective(assignments: Annotated[list[BoxAssignment], Len(8, 8)]) -> int:
    max_box_id = 0
    for i in range(1, N_ITEMS + 1):
        box_id = assignments[i].box_id
        if box_id > max_box_id:
            max_box_id = box_id
    return max_box_id

objective = calculated_objective_value

# --- constraints ---
def items_fit_exactly_in_boxes(
    items: Annotated[list[Item], Len(8, 8)],
    assignments: Annotated[list[BoxAssignment], Len(8, 8)]
) -> None:
    for i in range(1, N_ITEMS + 1):
        item_width = items[i].width
        item_height = items[i].height
        x_pos = assignments[i].x
        y_pos = assignments[i].y
        box_id = assignments[i].box_id

        # Ensure item fits within box dimensions
        assert x_pos + item_width <= BOX_WIDTH
        assert y_pos + item_height <= BOX_HEIGHT

items_fit_exactly_in_boxes(ITEMS, item_box_assignments)

# --- constraints ---
def no_overlap_between_items(
    assignments: Annotated[list[BoxAssignment], Len(8, 8)],
    items: Annotated[list[Item], Len(8, 8)]
) -> None:
    for i in range(1, N_ITEMS + 1):
        for j in range(i + 1, N_ITEMS + 1):
            # Only check overlap if both items are in the same box
            assert (assignments[i].box_id != assignments[j].box_id) or \
                   (assignments[i].x + items[i].width <= assignments[j].x) or \
                   (assignments[j].x + items[j].width <= assignments[i].x) or \
                   (assignments[i].y + items[i].height <= assignments[j].y) or \
                   (assignments[j].y + items[j].height <= assignments[i].y)

no_overlap_between_items(item_box_assignments, ITEMS)

# --- Auxiliary Variables ---
# Leave empty, if not required.
# --- constraints ---
def items_fit_exactly_in_boxes(
    assignments: Annotated[list[BoxAssignment], Len(8, 8)],
    items: Annotated[list[Item], Len(8, 8)],
    box_width: int,
    box_height: int
):
    for i in range(1, N_ITEMS + 1):
        item : Item = items[i]
        assignment : BoxAssignment = assignments[i]
        x_pos : int = assignment.x
        y_pos : int = assignment.y
        item_width : int = item.width
        item_height : int = item.height

# --- constraints ---
def no_overlap(
    assignments: Annotated[list[BoxAssignment], Len(8, 8)],
    items: Annotated[list[Item], Len(8, 8)]
):
    for i in range(1, N_ITEMS + 1):
        for j in range(i + 1, N_ITEMS + 1):
            # Check if both items are in the same box
            if assignments[i].box_id == assignments[j].box_id:
                # Check for non-overlapping rectangles
                assert (
                    assignments[i].x + items[i].width <= assignments[j].x or
                    assignments[j].x + items[j].width <= assignments[i].x or
                    assignments[i].y + items[i].height <= assignments[j].y or
                    assignments[j].y + items[j].height <= assignments[i].y
                )

objective = nr_used_boxes

# --- objective ---
def calculate_objective(assignments: Annotated[list[BoxAssignment], Len(8, 8)]) -> int:
    max_box_id = 0
    for i in range(1, N_ITEMS + 1):
        box_id = assignments[i].box_id
        if box_id > max_box_id:
            max_box_id = box_id
    return max_box_id

calculated_objective_value = calculate_objective(item_box_assignments)
objective = calculated_objective_value

# --- Auxiliary Variables ---
# Leave empty, if not required.
# --- constraints ---
def items_fit_exactly_in_boxes(
    assignments: Annotated[list[BoxAssignment], Len(8, 8)],
    items: Annotated[list[Item], Len(8, 8)],
    box_width: int,
    box_height: int
):
    for i in range(1, N_ITEMS + 1):
        item : Item = items[i]
        assignment : BoxAssignment = assignments[i]
        x_pos : int = assignment.x
        y_pos : int = assignment.y
        item_width : int = item.width
        item_height : int = item.height
        assert x_pos + item_width <= box_width
        assert y_pos + item_height <= box_height

items_fit_exactly_in_boxes(item_box_assignments, ITEMS, BOX_WIDTH, BOX_HEIGHT)

# --- constraints ---
def no_overlap(
    assignments: Annotated[list[BoxAssignment], Len(8, 8)],
    items: Annotated[list[Item], Len(8, 8)]
):
    for i in range(1, N_ITEMS + 1):
        for j in range(i + 1, N_ITEMS + 1):
            # Check if both items are in the same box
            if assignments[i].box_id == assignments[j].box_id:
                # Check for non-overlapping rectangles
                assert (
                    assignments[i].x + items[i].width <= assignments[j].x or
                    assignments[j].x + items[j].width <= assignments[i].x or
                    assignments[i].y + items[i].height <= assignments[j].y or
                    assignments[j].y + items[j].height <= assignments[i].y
                )

no_overlap(item_box_assignments, ITEMS)

# --- constraints ---
def each_item_in_one_box(
    assignments: Annotated[list[BoxAssignment], Len(8, 8)]
):
    for i in range(1, N_ITEMS + 1):
        box_id : int = assignments[i].box_id
        assert box_id >= 1
        assert box_id <= 8

each_item_in_one_box(item_box_assignments)

# --- objective ---
def calculate_objective(assignments: Annotated[list[BoxAssignment], Len(8, 8)]) -> int:
    max_box_id = 0

        if box_id > max_box_id:
            max_box_id = box_id
    return max_box_id

```python
from typing import Annotated
from pydantic import Field

# --- Objects ---
Item = DSRecord({
    "width": Annotated[int, Field(strict=True, ge=1, le=5)],
    "height": Annotated[int, Field(strict=True, ge=1, le=9)]
})

BoxAssignment = DSRecord({
    "box_id": Annotated[int, Field(strict=True, ge=1, le=8)],
    "x": Annotated[int, Field(strict=True, ge=0, le=5)],
    "y": Annotated[int, Field(strict=True, ge=0, le=12)]
})
```



# --- Constants ---
BOX_HEIGHT : int = 12
BOX_WIDTH : int = 5
ITEM1 : Item = {"width": 3, "height": 4}
ITEM2 : Item = {"width": 1, "height": 2}
ITEM3 : Item = {"width": 5, "height": 4}
ITEM4 : Item = {"width": 2, "height": 4}
ITEM5 : Item = {"width": 1, "height": 3}
ITEM6 : Item = {"width": 5, "height": 9}
ITEM7 : Item = {"width": 5, "height": 3}
ITEM8 : Item = {"width": 5, "height": 1}
ITEMS : Annotated[list[Item], Len(8, 8)] = [ITEM1, ITEM2, ITEM3, ITEM4, ITEM5, ITEM6, ITEM7, ITEM8]
N_ITEMS : int = 8
nr_used_boxes : Annotated[int, Field(strict=True, ge=1, le=8)]
item_box_assignments : Annotated[list[BoxAssignment], Len(8, 8)]
x_y_positions : Annotated[list[BoxAssignment], Len(8, 8)]


# -- Objective --


objective = nr_used_boxes

# --- objective ---
def calculate_objective(assignments: Annotated[list[BoxAssignment], Len(8, 8)]) -> int:
    max_box_id = 0
    for i in range(1, N_ITEMS + 1):
        box_id = assignments[i].box_id
        if box_id > max_box_id:
            max_box_id = box_id
    return max_box_id

calculated_objective_value = calculate_objective(item_box_assignments)
objective = calculated_objective_value

# --- Auxiliary Variables ---
# Leave empty, if not required.
# --- constraints ---
def fit_items_in_boxes(
    items: Annotated[list[Item], Len(8, 8)],
    assignments: Annotated[list[BoxAssignment], Len(8, 8)]
):
    for i in range(1, N_ITEMS + 1):
        item : Item = items[i]
        assignment : BoxAssignment = assignments[i]
        assert assignment.x + item.width <= BOX_WIDTH
        assert assignment.y + item.height <= BOX_HEIGHT

fit_items_in_boxes(ITEMS, item_box_assignments)

# --- Auxiliary Variables ---
# Leave empty, if not required.
# --- constraints ---
def no_overlap(
    items: Annotated[list[Item], Len(8, 8)],
    assignments: Annotated[list[BoxAssignment], Len(8, 8)]
):
    for i in range(1, N_ITEMS + 1):
        for j in range(i + 1, N_ITEMS + 1):
            assignment_i : BoxAssignment = assignments[i]
            assignment_j : BoxAssignment = assignments[j]
            item_i : Item = items[i]
            item_j : Item = items[j]

            # Check if items are in the same box
            same_box : bool = assignment_i.box_id == assignment_j.box_id

            # Check for non-overlapping in x-axis
            no_overlap_x : bool = (assignment_i.x + item_i.width <= assignment_j.x) or (assignment_j.x + item_j.width <= assignment_i.x)

            # Check for non-overlapping in y-axis
            no_overlap_y : bool = (assignment_i.y + item_i.height <= assignment_j.y) or (assignment_j.y + item_j.height <= assignment_i.y)

            # If in the same box, they must not overlap
            assert not same_box or no_overlap_x or no_overlap_y

no_overlap(ITEMS, item_box_assignments)

        assert assignment.box_id <= 8

# --- objective ---
def calculate_objective(assignments: Annotated[list[int], Len(8, 8)]) -> int:
    max_box = 0
    for i in range(1, N_ITEMS + 1):
        if assignments[i] > max_box:
            max_box = assignments[i]
    return max_box

calculated_objective_value = calculate_objective(item_box_assignments)
objective = calculated_objective_value

# --- constraints ---
def fit_items_in_box(
    items: Annotated[list[Item], Len(8, 8)],
    positions: Annotated[list[Position], Len(8, 8)],
    assignments: Annotated[list[int], Len(8, 8)],
    box_width: int,
    box_height: int
):
    for i in range(1, N_ITEMS + 1):
        item: Item = items[i]
        pos: Position = positions[i]
        box_id: int = assignments[i]

        # Ensure item fits within the box dimensions
        assert pos.x + item.width <= box_width
        assert pos.y + item.height <= box_height
        assert pos.x >= 0
        assert pos.y >= 0

# --- Auxiliary Variables ---
# Leave empty, if not required.
# --- constraints ---
def no_overlap(
    items: Annotated[list[Item], Len(8, 8)],
    positions: Annotated[list[Position], Len(8, 8)],
    assignments: Annotated[list[int], Len(8, 8)]
):
    for i in range(1, N_ITEMS + 1):
        for j in range(i + 1, N_ITEMS + 1):
            if assignments[i] == assignments[j]:
                item1: Item = items[i]
                pos1: Position = positions[i]
                item2: Item = items[j]
                pos2: Position = positions[j]

                # Check if rectangles overlap
                assert not (
                    pos1.x < pos2.x + item2.width and
                    pos1.x + item1.width > pos2.x and
                    pos1.y < pos2.y + item2.height and
                    pos1.y + item1.height > pos2.y
                )

# --- objective ---
def calculate_objective(assignments: Annotated[list[int], Len(8, 8)]) -> int:
    max_box = 0
    for i in range(1, N_ITEMS + 1):
        if assignments[i] > max_box:
            max_box = assignments[i]
    return max_box

calculated_objective_value = calculate_objective(item_box_assignments)
objective = calculated_objective_value

# -- Constraints --


# --- constraints ---
def fit_items_in_box(
    items: Annotated[list[Item], Len(8, 8)],
    positions: Annotated[list[Position], Len(8, 8)],
    assignments: Annotated[list[int], Len(8, 8)],
    box_width: int,
    box_height: int
):
    for i in range(1, N_ITEMS + 1):
        item: Item = items[i]
        pos: Position = positions[i]
        box_id: int = assignments[i]

        # Ensure item fits within the box dimensions
        assert pos.x + item.width <= box_width
        assert pos.y + item.height <= box_height
        assert pos.x >= 0
        assert pos.y >= 0

fit_items_in_box(ITEMS, x_y_positions, item_box_assignments, BOX_WIDTH, BOX_HEIGHT)

# --- Auxiliary Variables ---
# Leave empty, if not required.
# --- constraints ---
def no_overlap(
    items: Annotated[list[Item], Len(8, 8)],
    positions: Annotated[list[Position], Len(8, 8)],
    assignments: Annotated[list[int], Len(8, 8)]
):
    for i in range(1, N_ITEMS + 1):
        for j in range(i + 1, N_ITEMS + 1):
            if assignments[i] == assignments[j]:
                item1: Item = items[i]
                pos1: Position = positions[i]
                item2: Item = items[j]
                pos2: Position = positions[j]

                # Check if rectangles overlap
                assert not (
                    pos1.x < pos2.x + item2.width and
                    pos1.x + item1.width > pos2.x and
                    pos1.y < pos2.y + item2.height and
                    pos1.y + item1.height > pos2.y
                )

no_overlap(ITEMS, x_y_positions, item_box_assignments)

# Leave empty, if not required.
# --- constraints ---
def no_overlap(
    assignments: Annotated[list[BoxAssignment], Len(8, 8)],
    items: Annotated[list[Item], Len(8, 8)]
):
    for i in range(1, N_ITEMS + 1):
        for j in range(i + 1, N_ITEMS + 1):
            assignment_i: BoxAssignment = assignments[i]
            assignment_j: BoxAssignment = assignments[j]
            item_i: Item = items[i]
            item_j: Item = items[j]

            # Check if items are in the same box
            if assignment_i.box_id == assignment_j.box_id:
                # Check for overlap on x-axis
                x_overlap: bool = not (
                    assignment_i.x + item_i.width <= assignment_j.x or
                    assignment_j.x + item_j.width <= assignment_i.x
                )

                # Check for overlap on y-axis
                y_overlap: bool = not (
                    assignment_i.y + item_i.height <= assignment_j.y or
                    assignment_j.y + item_j.height <= assignment_i.y
                )

                # Assert that there is no overlap
                assert not (x_overlap and y_overlap)

```python
Item = DSRecord({
    "width": Annotated[int, Field(strict=True, ge=1, le=5)],
    "height": Annotated[int, Field(strict=True, ge=1, le=9)]
})

BoxAssignment = DSRecord({
    "box_id": Annotated[int, Field(strict=True, ge=1, le=8)],
    "x": Annotated[int, Field(strict=True, ge=0, le=5)],
    "y": Annotated[int, Field(strict=True, ge=0, le=12)]
})
```

# --- Constants ---

ITEM3 : Item = {"width": 5, "height": 4}
ITEM4 : Item = {"width": 2, "height": 4}
ITEM5 : Item = {"width": 1, "height": 3}
ITEM6 : Item = {"width": 5, "height": 9}
ITEM7 : Item = {"width": 5, "height": 3}
ITEM8 : Item = {"width": 5, "height": 1}
ITEMS : Annotated[list[Item], Len(8, 8)] = [ITEM1, ITEM2, ITEM3, ITEM4, ITEM5, ITEM6, ITEM7, ITEM8]

nr_used_boxes : Annotated[int, Field(strict=True, ge=1, le=8)]
item_box_assignments : Annotated[list[BoxAssignment], Len(8, 8)]

# -- Objective --


objective = nr_used_boxes

# --- objective ---
def calculate_objective(assignments: Annotated[list[BoxAssignment], Len(8, 8)]) -> int:
    max_box_id = 0
    for i in range(1, N_ITEMS + 1):
        box_id = assignments[i].box_id
        if box_id > max_box_id:
            max_box_id = box_id
    return max_box_id

calculated_objective_value = calculate_objective(item_box_assignments)
objective = calculated_objective_value

# -- Constraints --


# --- Auxiliary Variables ---
# Leave empty, if not required.
# --- constraints ---
def fit_items_in_boxes(
    items: Annotated[list[Item], Len(8, 8)],
    assignments: Annotated[list[BoxAssignment], Len(8, 8)],
    box_width: int,
    box_height: int
):
    for i in range(1, N_ITEMS + 1):
        item: Item = items[i]
        assignment: BoxAssignment = assignments[i]
        assert assignment.x + item.width <= box_width
        assert assignment.y + item.height <= box_height

fit_items_in_boxes(ITEMS, item_box_assignments, BOX_WIDTH, BOX_HEIGHT)

# --- Auxiliary Variables ---
# Leave empty, if not required.
# --- constraints ---
def no_overlap(
    assignments: Annotated[list[BoxAssignment], Len(8, 8)],
    items: Annotated[list[Item], Len(8, 8)]
):
    for i in range(1, N_ITEMS + 1):
        for j in range(i + 1, N_ITEMS + 1):
            assignment_i: BoxAssignment = assignments[i]
            assignment_j: BoxAssignment = assignments[j]
            item_i: Item = items[i]
            item_j: Item = items[j]

            # Check if items are in the same box
            if assignment_i.box_id == assignment_j.box_id:
                # Check for overlap on x-axis
                x_overlap: bool = not (
                    assignment_i.x + item_i.width <= assignment_j.x or
                    assignment_j.x + item_j.width <= assignment_i.x
                )

                # Check for overlap on y-axis
                y_overlap: bool = not (
                    assignment_i.y + item_i.height <= assignment_j.y or
                    assignment_j.y + item_j.height <= assignment_i.y
                )

                # Assert that there is no overlap
                assert not (x_overlap and y_overlap)

no_overlap(item_box_assignments, ITEMS)

def ensure_item_box_assignment_validity(
    assignments: Annotated[list[BoxAssignment], Len(8, 8)]
):
    for i in range(1, N_ITEMS + 1):
        assignment: BoxAssignment = assignments[i]
        assert assignment.box_id >= 1
        assert assignment.box_id <= 8
        assert assignment.x >= 0
        assert assignment.x <= 5
        assert assignment.y >= 0
        assert assignment.y <= 12

# --- objective ---
def calculate_objective(assignments: Annotated[list[BoxAssignment], Len(8, 8)]) -> int:
    max_box_id = 0
    for i in range(1, N_ITEMS + 1):
        box_id = assignments[i].box_id
        if box_id > max_box_id:
            max_box_id = box_id
    return max_box_id

calculated_objective_value = calculate_objective(item_box_assignments)
objective = calculated_objective_value

# --- Auxiliary Variables ---
# Leave empty, if not required.
# --- constraints ---
def fit_items_in_boxes(
    items: Annotated[list[Item], Len(8, 8)],
    assignments: Annotated[list[BoxAssignment], Len(8, 8)],
    box_width: int,
    box_height: int
):
    for i in range(1, N_ITEMS + 1):
        item: Item = items[i]
        assignment: BoxAssignment = assignments[i]
        assert assignment.x + item.width <= box_width
        assert assignment.y + item.height <= box_height

# --- constraints ---
def no_overlap(
    assignments: Annotated[list[BoxAssignment], Len(8, 8)],
    items: Annotated[list[Item], Len(8, 8)]
):
    for i in range(1, N_ITEMS + 1):
        for j in range(i + 1, N_ITEMS + 1):
            # Check if items are in the same box
            assert assignments[i].box_id != assignments[j].box_id or \
                   (assignments[i].x + items[i].width <= assignments[j].x) or \

# -- Objects --


```python
from typing import Annotated
from pydantic import Field

# --- Objects ---
Item = DSRecord({
    "width": Annotated[int, Field(strict=True, ge=1, le=5)],
    "height": Annotated[int, Field(strict=True, ge=1, le=9)]
})

BoxAssignment = DSRecord({
    "box_id": Annotated[int, Field(strict=True, ge=1, le=8)],
    "x": Annotated[int, Field(strict=True, ge=0, le=5)],
    "y": Annotated[int, Field(strict=True, ge=0, le=12)]
})
```



# --- Constants ---
BOX_HEIGHT : int = 12
BOX_WIDTH : int = 5
ITEM1 : Item = {"width": 3, "height": 4}
ITEM2 : Item = {"width": 1, "height": 2}
ITEM3 : Item = {"width": 5, "height": 4}
ITEM4 : Item = {"width": 2, "height": 4}
ITEM5 : Item = {"width": 1, "height": 3}
ITEM6 : Item = {"width": 5, "height": 9}
ITEM7 : Item = {"width": 5, "height": 3}
ITEM8 : Item = {"width": 5, "height": 1}
ITEMS : Annotated[list[Item], Len(8, 8)] = [ITEM1, ITEM2, ITEM3, ITEM4, ITEM5, ITEM6, ITEM7, ITEM8]
N_ITEMS : int = 8
nr_used_boxes : Annotated[int, Field(strict=True, ge=1, le=8)]
item_box_assignments : Annotated[list[BoxAssignment], Len(8, 8)]
x_y_positions : Annotated[list[BoxAssignment], Len(8, 8)]


# -- Objective --


objective = nr_used_boxes

# --- objective ---
def calculate_objective(assignments: Annotated[list[BoxAssignment], Len(8, 8)]) -> int:
    max_box_id = 0
    for i in range(1, N_ITEMS + 1):
        box_id = assignments[i].box_id
        if box_id > max_box_id:
            max_box_id = box_id
    return max_box_id

calculated_objective_value = calculate_objective(item_box_assignments)
objective = calculated_objective_value

# -- Constraints --


# --- Auxiliary Variables ---
# Leave empty, if not required.
# --- constraints ---
def fit_items_in_boxes(
    items: Annotated[list[Item], Len(8, 8)],
    assignments: Annotated[list[BoxAssignment], Len(8, 8)],
    box_width: int,
    box_height: int
):
    for i in range(1, N_ITEMS + 1):
        item: Item = items[i]
        assignment: BoxAssignment = assignments[i]
        assert assignment.x + item.width <= box_width
        assert assignment.y + item.height <= box_height

fit_items_in_boxes(ITEMS, item_box_assignments, BOX_WIDTH, BOX_HEIGHT)

# --- constraints ---
def no_overlap(
    assignments: Annotated[list[BoxAssignment], Len(8, 8)],
    items: Annotated[list[Item], Len(8, 8)]
):
    for i in range(1, N_ITEMS + 1):
        for j in range(i + 1, N_ITEMS + 1):
            # Check if items are in the same box
            assert assignments[i].box_id != assignments[j].box_id or \
                   (assignments[i].x + items[i].width <= assignments[j].x) or \
                   (assignments[j].x + items[j].width <= assignments[i].x) or \
                   (assignments[i].y + items[i].height <= assignments[j].y) or \
                   (assignments[j].y + items[j].height <= assignments[i].y)

# --- objective ---
def calculate_objective(assignments: Annotated[list[BoxAssignment], Len(8, 8)]) -> int:
    max_box_id = 0
    for i in range(1, N_ITEMS + 1):
        box_id = assignments[i].box_id
        if box_id > max_box_id:
            max_box_id = box_id
    return max_box_id

calculated_objective_value = calculate_objective(item_box_assignments)
objective = calculated_objective_value

def items_fit_exactly_in_boxes(

```python
from typing import Annotated
from pydantic import Field

# --- Objects ---
Item = DSRecord({
    "width": Annotated[int, Field(strict=True, ge=1, le=5)],
    "height": Annotated[int, Field(strict=True, ge=1, le=9)]
})

BoxAssignment = DSRecord({
    "box_id": Annotated[int, Field(strict=True, ge=1, le=8)],
    "x": Annotated[int, Field(strict=True, ge=0, le=5)],
    "y": Annotated[int, Field(strict=True, ge=0, le=12)]
})
```

objective = nr_used_boxes

# --- objective ---
def calculate_objective(assignments: Annotated[list[BoxAssignment], Len(8, 8)]) -> int:
    max_box_id = 0
    for i in range(1, N_ITEMS + 1):
        box_id = assignments[i].box_id
        if box_id > max_box_id:
            max_box_id = box_id
    return max_box_id

calculated_objective_value = calculate_objective(item_box_assignments)
objective = calculated_objective_value

# -- Constraints --


# --- Auxiliary Variables ---
# Leave empty, if not required.
# --- constraints ---
def items_fit_exactly_in_boxes(
    items: Annotated[list[Item], Len(8, 8)],
    assignments: Annotated[list[BoxAssignment], Len(8, 8)]
) -> None:
    for i in range(1, N_ITEMS + 1):
        item_width = items[i].width
        item_height = items[i].height
        x_pos = assignments[i].x
        y_pos = assignments[i].y

        assert x_pos + item_width <= BOX_WIDTH
        assert y_pos + item_height <= BOX_HEIGHT

items_fit_exactly_in_boxes(ITEMS, item_box_assignments)

# Leave empty, if not required.
# --- constraints ---
def items_fit_exactly_in_boxes(
    items: Annotated[list[Item], Len(8, 8)],
    assignments: Annotated[list[BoxAssignment], Len(8, 8)],
    box_width: int,
    box_height: int
):
    for i in range(1, N_ITEMS + 1):
        item : Item = items[i]
        assignment : BoxAssignment = assignments[i]
        x_end : int = assignment.x + item.width
        y_end : int = assignment.y + item.height
        assert assignment.x >= 0
        assert assignment.y >= 0
        assert x_end <= box_width
        assert y_end <= box_height

# --- Auxiliary Variables ---
# Leave empty, if not required.
# --- constraints ---
def no_overlap(
    assignments: Annotated[list[BoxAssignment], Len(8, 8)],
    items: Annotated[list[Item], Len(8, 8)]
):
    for i in range(1, N_ITEMS + 1):
        for j in range(i + 1, N_ITEMS + 1):
            assignment_i : BoxAssignment = assignments[i]
            assignment_j : BoxAssignment = assignments[j]
            item_i : Item = items[i]
            item_j : Item = items[j]

            # Calculate boundaries for item i
            x1_i : int = assignment_i.x
            x2_i : int = assignment_i.x + item_i.width
            y1_i : int = assignment_i.y
            y2_i : int = assignment_i.y + item_i.height

            # Calculate boundaries for item j
            x1_j : int = assignment_j.x
            x2_j : int = assignment_j.x + item_j.width
            y1_j : int = assignment_j.y
            y2_j : int = assignment_j.y + item_j.height

            # Check if boxes are different
            same_box : bool = assignment_i.box_id == assignment_j.box_id

            # Overlap conditions: NOT (no overlap)
            # No overlap means: one rectangle is to the left, right, above, or below the other
            no_overlap_condition : bool = (
                x2_i <= x1_j or  # i is to the left of j
                x2_j <= x1_i or  # j is to the left of i
                y2_i <= y1_j or  # i is below j
                y2_j <= y1_i     # j is below i
            )

            # If in the same box, they must not overlap
            assert not same_box or no_overlap_condition

no_overlap(item_box_assignments, ITEMS)

```python
from typing import Annotated
from pydantic import Field

# --- Objects ---
Item = DSRecord({
    "width": Annotated[int, Field(strict=True, ge=1, le=5)],
    "height": Annotated[int, Field(strict=True, ge=1, le=9)]
})

BoxAssignment = DSRecord({
    "box_id": Annotated[int, Field(strict=True, ge=1, le=8)],
    "x": Annotated[int, Field(strict=True, ge=0, le=5)],
    "y": Annotated[int, Field(strict=True, ge=0, le=12)]
})
```



# --- Constants ---
BOX_HEIGHT : int = 12
BOX_WIDTH : int = 5
ITEM1 : Item = {"width": 3, "height": 4}
ITEM2 : Item = {"width": 1, "height": 2}
ITEM3 : Item = {"width": 5, "height": 4}
ITEM4 : Item = {"width": 2, "height": 4}
ITEM5 : Item = {"width": 1, "height": 3}
ITEM6 : Item = {"width": 5, "height": 9}
ITEM7 : Item = {"width": 5, "height": 3}
ITEM8 : Item = {"width": 5, "height": 1}
ITEMS : Annotated[list[Item], Len(8, 8)] = [ITEM1, ITEM2, ITEM3, ITEM4, ITEM5, ITEM6, ITEM7, ITEM8]
N_ITEMS : int = 8
nr_used_boxes : Annotated[int, Field(strict=True, ge=1, le=8)]
item_box_assignments : Annotated[list[BoxAssignment], Len(8, 8)]
x_y_positions : Annotated[list[BoxAssignment], Len(8, 8)]


# -- Objective --


objective = nr_used_boxes

# --- objective ---
def calculate_objective(assignments: Annotated[list[BoxAssignment], Len(8, 8)]) -> int:
    max_box_id = 0
    for i in range(1, N_ITEMS + 1):
        box_id = assignments[i].box_id
        if box_id > max_box_id:
            max_box_id = box_id
    return max_box_id

calculated_objective_value = calculate_objective(item_box_assignments)
objective = calculated_objective_value

# -- Constraints --


# --- Auxiliary Variables ---
# Leave empty, if not required.
# --- constraints ---
def items_fit_exactly_in_boxes(
    items: Annotated[list[Item], Len(8, 8)],
    assignments: Annotated[list[BoxAssignment], Len(8, 8)],
    box_width: int,
    box_height: int
):
    for i in range(1, N_ITEMS + 1):
        item : Item = items[i]
        assignment : BoxAssignment = assignments[i]
        x_end : int = assignment.x + item.width
        y_end : int = assignment.y + item.height
        assert assignment.x >= 0
        assert assignment.y >= 0
        assert x_end <= box_width
        assert y_end <= box_height

items_fit_exactly_in_boxes(ITEMS, item_box_assignments, BOX_WIDTH, BOX_HEIGHT)

# --- Auxiliary Variables ---
# Leave empty, if not required.
# --- constraints ---
def no_overlap(
    assignments: Annotated[list[BoxAssignment], Len(8, 8)],
    items: Annotated[list[Item], Len(8, 8)]
):
    for i in range(1, N_ITEMS + 1):
        for j in range(i + 1, N_ITEMS + 1):
            assignment_i : BoxAssignment = assignments[i]
            assignment_j : BoxAssignment = assignments[j]
            item_i : Item = items[i]
            item_j : Item = items[j]

            # Calculate boundaries for item i
            x1_i : int = assignment_i.x
            x2_i : int = assignment_i.x + item_i.width
            y1_i : int = assignment_i.y
            y2_i : int = assignment_i.y + item_i.height

            # Calculate boundaries for item j
            x1_j : int = assignment_j.x
            x2_j : int = assignment_j.x + item_j.width
            y1_j : int = assignment_j.y
            y2_j : int = assignment_j.y + item_j.height

            # Check if boxes are different
            same_box : bool = assignment_i.box_id == assignment_j.box_id

            # Overlap conditions: NOT (no overlap)
            # No overlap means: one rectangle is to the left, right, above, or below the other
            no_overlap_condition : bool = (
                x2_i <= x1_j or  # i is to the left of j
                x2_j <= x1_i or  # j is to the left of i
                y2_i <= y1_j or  # i is below j
                y2_j <= y1_i     # j is below i
            )

            # If in the same box, they must not overlap
            assert not same_box or no_overlap_condition

no_overlap(item_box_assignments, ITEMS)

):
    for i in range(1, N_ITEMS + 1):
        box_id = assignments[i].box_id
        assert box_id >= 1
        assert box_id <= 8

# --- objective ---
def calculate_objective(assignments: Annotated[list[BoxAssignment], Len(8, 8)]) -> int:
    max_box_id = 0
    for i in range(1, N_ITEMS + 1):
        box_id = assignments[i].box_id
        if box_id > max_box_id:
            max_box_id = box_id
    return max_box_id

# --- Auxiliary Variables ---
# Leave empty, if not required.
# --- constraints ---
def no_item_overlap(
    items: Annotated[list[Item], Len(8, 8)],
    assignments: Annotated[list[BoxAssignment], Len(8, 8)],
    box_width: int,
    box_height: int
):
    for i in range(1, N_ITEMS + 1):
        for j in range(i + 1, N_ITEMS + 1):
            assignment_i : BoxAssignment = assignments[i]
            assignment_j : BoxAssignment = assignments[j]
            item_i : Item = items[i]
            item_j : Item = items[j]

            # Check if items are in the same box
            same_box : bool = assignment_i.box_id == assignment_j.box_id

            # Calculate boundaries for item i
            right_i : int = assignment_i.x + item_i.width
            top_i : int = assignment_i.y + item_i.height

            # Calculate boundaries for item j
            right_j : int = assignment_j.x + item_j.width
            top_j : int = assignment_j.y + item_j.height

            # Overlap condition: NOT (left >= right OR right <= left OR bottom >= top OR top <= bottom)
            not_overlap : bool = (
                assignment_i.x >= right_j or
                assignment_j.x >= right_i or
                assignment_i.y >= top_j or
                assignment_j.y >= top_i
            )

            # If items are in the same box, they must not overlap
            assert not same_box or not_overlap

no_item_overlap(ITEMS, item_box_assignments, BOX_WIDTH, BOX_HEIGHT)

```python
from typing import Annotated
from pydantic import Field

# --- Objects ---
Item = DSRecord({
    "width": Annotated[int, Field(strict=True, ge=1, le=5)],
    "height": Annotated[int, Field(strict=True, ge=1, le=9)]
})

BoxAssignment = DSRecord({
    "box_id": Annotated[int, Field(strict=True, ge=1, le=8)],
    "x": Annotated[int, Field(strict=True, ge=0, le=5)],
    "y": Annotated[int, Field(strict=True, ge=0, le=12)]
})
```



# --- Constants ---
BOX_HEIGHT : int = 12
BOX_WIDTH : int = 5
ITEM1 : Item = {"width": 3, "height": 4}
ITEM2 : Item = {"width": 1, "height": 2}
ITEM3 : Item = {"width": 5, "height": 4}
ITEM4 : Item = {"width": 2, "height": 4}
ITEM5 : Item = {"width": 1, "height": 3}
ITEM6 : Item = {"width": 5, "height": 9}
ITEM7 : Item = {"width": 5, "height": 3}
ITEM8 : Item = {"width": 5, "height": 1}
ITEMS : Annotated[list[Item], Len(8, 8)] = [ITEM1, ITEM2, ITEM3, ITEM4, ITEM5, ITEM6, ITEM7, ITEM8]
N_ITEMS : int = 8
nr_used_boxes : Annotated[int, Field(strict=True, ge=1, le=8)]
item_box_assignments : Annotated[list[BoxAssignment], Len(8, 8)]
x_y_positions : Annotated[list[BoxAssignment], Len(8, 8)]

objective = nr_used_boxes

# --- objective ---
def calculate_objective(assignments: Annotated[list[BoxAssignment], Len(8, 8)]) -> int:
    max_box_id = 0
    for i in range(1, N_ITEMS + 1):
        box_id = assignments[i].box_id
        if box_id > max_box_id:
            max_box_id = box_id
    return max_box_id

calculated_objective_value = calculate_objective(item_box_assignments)
objective = calculated_objective_value

# --- Auxiliary Variables ---
# Leave empty, if not required.
# --- constraints ---
def items_fit_exactly_in_boxes(
    items: Annotated[list[Item], Len(8, 8)],
    assignments: Annotated[list[BoxAssignment], Len(8, 8)],
    box_width: int,
    box_height: int
):
    for i in range(1, N_ITEMS + 1):
        item : Item = items[i]
        assignment : BoxAssignment = assignments[i]
        assert assignment.x + item.width <= box_width
        assert assignment.y + item.height <= box_height

items_fit_exactly_in_boxes(ITEMS, item_box_assignments, BOX_WIDTH, BOX_HEIGHT)

# --- Auxiliary Variables ---
# Leave empty, if not required.
# --- constraints ---
def no_item_overlap(
    items: Annotated[list[Item], Len(8, 8)],
    assignments: Annotated[list[BoxAssignment], Len(8, 8)],
    box_width: int,
    box_height: int
):
    for i in range(1, N_ITEMS + 1):
        for j in range(i + 1, N_ITEMS + 1):
            assignment_i : BoxAssignment = assignments[i]
            assignment_j : BoxAssignment = assignments[j]
            item_i : Item = items[i]
            item_j : Item = items[j]

            # Check if items are in the same box
            same_box : bool = assignment_i.box_id == assignment_j.box_id

            # Calculate boundaries for item i
            right_i : int = assignment_i.x + item_i.width
            top_i : int = assignment_i.y + item_i.height

            # Calculate boundaries for item j
            right_j : int = assignment_j.x + item_j.width
            top_j : int = assignment_j.y + item_j.height

            # Overlap condition: NOT (left >= right OR right <= left OR bottom >= top OR top <= bottom)
            not_overlap : bool = (
                assignment_i.x >= right_j or
                assignment_j.x >= right_i or
                assignment_i.y >= top_j or
                assignment_j.y >= top_i
            )

            # If items are in the same box, they must not overlap
            assert not same_box or not_overlap

no_item_overlap(ITEMS, item_box_assignments, BOX_WIDTH, BOX_HEIGHT)

        box_id = assignments[i].box_id
        assert box_id >= 1
        assert box_id <= 8

# --- Auxiliary Variables ---
# No additional auxiliary variables needed
# --- constraints ---
def pack_items_in_boxes(
    items: Annotated[list[Item], Len(8, 8)],
    item_box_assignments: Annotated[list[int], Len(8, 8)],
    x_y_positions: Annotated[list[Position], Len(8, 8)],
    nr_used_boxes: int
) -> None:
    # Each item must be assigned to a valid box (1 to nr_used_boxes)
    for i in range(1, N_ITEMS + 1):
        assert 1 <= item_box_assignments[i] <= nr_used_boxes

    # Each item's dimensions must fit within the box dimensions
    for i in range(1, N_ITEMS + 1):
        item : Item = items[i]
        assert item.width <= BOX_WIDTH
        assert item.height <= BOX_HEIGHT

    # Positions must be within box boundaries
    for i in range(1, N_ITEMS + 1):
        pos : Position = x_y_positions[i]
        assert pos.x >= 0
        assert pos.y >= 0
        assert pos.x + items[i].width <= BOX_WIDTH
        assert pos.y + items[i].height <= BOX_HEIGHT

def ensure_no_overlap_and_valid_positioning(
    items: Annotated[list[Item], Len(8, 8)],
    item_box_assignments: Annotated[list[int], Len(8, 8)],
    x_y_positions: Annotated[list[Position], Len(8, 8)],
    nr_used_boxes: int
) -> None:
    # Each item must be assigned to a valid box (1 to nr_used_boxes)
    for i in range(1, N_ITEMS + 1):
        assert 1 <= item_box_assignments[i] <= nr_used_boxes

    # Each item's dimensions must fit within the box dimensions
    for i in range(1, N_ITEMS + 1):
        item : Item = items[i]
        assert item.width <= BOX_WIDTH
        assert item.height <= BOX_HEIGHT

    # Positions must be within box boundaries
    for i in range(1, N_ITEMS + 1):
        pos : Position = x_y_positions[i]
        assert pos.x >= 0
        assert pos.y >= 0
        assert pos.x + items[i].width <= BOX_WIDTH
        assert pos.y + items[i].height <= BOX_HEIGHT

    # Ensure no overlapping between items in the same box
    for i in range(1, N_ITEMS + 1):
        for j in range(i + 1, N_ITEMS + 1):
            # Only check for overlap if both items are in the same box
            if item_box_assignments[i] == item_box_assignments[j]:
                pos_i : Position = x_y_positions[i]
                pos_j : Position = x_y_positions[j]
                item_i : Item = items[i]
                item_j : Item = items[j]
                # Check if rectangles overlap
                assert not (
                    (pos_i.x < pos_j.x + item_j.width) and
                    (pos_j.x < pos_i.x + item_i.width) and
                    (pos_i.y < pos_j.y + item_j.height) and
                    (pos_j.y < pos_i.y + item_i.height)
                )

def ensure_no_overlap(
    items: Annotated[list[Item], Len(8, 8)],
    item_box_assignments: Annotated[list[int], Len(8, 8)],
    x_y_positions: Annotated[list[Position], Len(8, 8)],
    nr_used_boxes: int
) -> None:

# --- objective ---
def calculate_objective(assignments: Annotated[list[BoxAssignment], Len(8, 8)]) -> int:
    max_box_id = 0
    for i in range(1, N_ITEMS + 1):
        box_id = assignments[i].box_id
        if box_id > max_box_id:
            max_box_id = box_id
    return max_box_id

# --- Auxiliary Variables ---
# Leave empty, if not required.
# --- constraints ---
def no_overlap(
    assignments: Annotated[list[BoxAssignment], Len(8, 8)],
    items: Annotated[list[Item], Len(8, 8)]
):
    for i in range(1, N_ITEMS + 1):
        for j in range(i + 1, N_ITEMS + 1):
            assignment_i: BoxAssignment = assignments[i]
            assignment_j: BoxAssignment = assignments[j]
            item_i: Item = items[i]
            item_j: Item = items[j]

            # Check if items are in the same box
            if assignment_i.box_id == assignment_j.box_id:
                # Check for overlap on x-axis
                x_overlap: bool = not (
                    assignment_i.x + item_i.width <= assignment_j.x or
                    assignment_j.x + item_j.width <= assignment_i.x
                )

                # Check for overlap on y-axis
                y_overlap: bool = not (
                    assignment_i.y + item_i.height <= assignment_j.y or
                    assignment_j.y + item_j.height <= assignment_i.y
                )

                # If both overlaps are true, there is an overlap
                assert not (x_overlap and y_overlap)

no_overlap(item_box_assignments, ITEMS)

```python
from typing import Annotated
from pydantic import Field

# --- Objects ---
Item = DSRecord({
    "width": Annotated[int, Field(strict=True, ge=1, le=5)],
    "height": Annotated[int, Field(strict=True, ge=1, le=9)]
})

BoxAssignment = DSRecord({
    "box_id": Annotated[int, Field(strict=True, ge=1, le=8)],
    "x": Annotated[int, Field(strict=True, ge=0, le=5)],
    "y": Annotated[int, Field(strict=True, ge=0, le=12)]
})
```



# --- Constants ---
BOX_HEIGHT : int = 12
BOX_WIDTH : int = 5
ITEM1 : Item = {"width": 3, "height": 4}
ITEM2 : Item = {"width": 1, "height": 2}
ITEM3 : Item = {"width": 5, "height": 4}
ITEM4 : Item = {"width": 2, "height": 4}
ITEM5 : Item = {"width": 1, "height": 3}
ITEM6 : Item = {"width": 5, "height": 9}
ITEM7 : Item = {"width": 5, "height": 3}
ITEM8 : Item = {"width": 5, "height": 1}
ITEMS : Annotated[list[Item], Len(8, 8)] = [ITEM1, ITEM2, ITEM3, ITEM4, ITEM5, ITEM6, ITEM7, ITEM8]
N_ITEMS : int = 8
nr_used_boxes : Annotated[int, Field(strict=True, ge=1, le=8)]
item_box_assignments : Annotated[list[BoxAssignment], Len(8, 8)]
x_y_positions : Annotated[list[BoxAssignment], Len(8, 8)]


# -- Objective --


objective = nr_used_boxes

# --- objective ---
def calculate_objective(assignments: Annotated[list[BoxAssignment], Len(8, 8)]) -> int:
    max_box_id = 0
    for i in range(1, N_ITEMS + 1):
        box_id = assignments[i].box_id
        if box_id > max_box_id:
            max_box_id = box_id
    return max_box_id

calculated_objective_value = calculate_objective(item_box_assignments)
objective = calculated_objective_value

# -- Constraints --


# --- Auxiliary Variables ---
# Leave empty, if not required.
# --- constraints ---
def fit_items_in_box(
    items: Annotated[list[Item], Len(8, 8)],
    assignments: Annotated[list[BoxAssignment], Len(8, 8)],
    box_width: int,
    box_height: int
):
    for i in range(1, N_ITEMS + 1):
        item: Item = items[i]
        assignment: BoxAssignment = assignments[i]
        assert assignment.x + item.width <= box_width
        assert assignment.y + item.height <= box_height

fit_items_in_box(ITEMS, item_box_assignments, BOX_WIDTH, BOX_HEIGHT)

# --- Auxiliary Variables ---
# Leave empty, if not required.
# --- constraints ---
def no_overlap(
    assignments: Annotated[list[BoxAssignment], Len(8, 8)],
    items: Annotated[list[Item], Len(8, 8)]
):
    for i in range(1, N_ITEMS + 1):
        for j in range(i + 1, N_ITEMS + 1):
            assignment_i: BoxAssignment = assignments[i]
            assignment_j: BoxAssignment = assignments[j]
            item_i: Item = items[i]
            item_j: Item = items[j]

            # Check if items are in the same box
            if assignment_i.box_id == assignment_j.box_id:
                # Check for overlap on x-axis
                x_overlap: bool = not (
                    assignment_i.x + item_i.width <= assignment_j.x or
                    assignment_j.x + item_j.width <= assignment_i.x
                )

                # Check for overlap on y-axis
                y_overlap: bool = not (
                    assignment_i.y + item_i.height <= assignment_j.y or
                    assignment_j.y + item_j.height <= assignment_i.y
                )

                # If both overlaps are true, there is an overlap
                assert not (x_overlap and y_overlap)

no_overlap(item_box_assignments, ITEMS)

# --- Auxiliary Variables ---
# Leave empty, if not required.
# --- constraints ---
def ensure_item_in_one_box(
    assignments: Annotated[list[BoxAssignment], Len(8, 8)]
):
    for i in range(1, N_ITEMS + 1):
        assert assignments[i].box_id >= 1
        assert assignments[i].box_id <= 8

ensure_item_in_one_box(item_box_assignments)

# --- objective ---
def calculate_objective(assignments: Annotated[list[BoxAssignment], Len(8, 8)]) -> int:
    max_box_id = 0
    for i in range(1, N_ITEMS + 1):
        box_id = assignments[i].box_id
        if box_id > max_box_id:
            max_box_id = box_id
    return max_box_id

calculated_objective_value = calculate_objective(item_box_assignments)
objective = calculated_objective_value

# --- constraints ---
def no_overlap(
    items: Annotated[list[Item], Len(8, 8)],
    assignments: Annotated[list[BoxAssignment], Len(8, 8)]
):
    for i in range(1, N_ITEMS + 1):
        for j in range(i + 1, N_ITEMS + 1):

# -- Objective --


objective = nr_used_boxes

# --- objective ---
def calculate_objective(assignments: Annotated[list[BoxAssignment], Len(8, 8)]) -> int:
    max_box_id = 0
    for i in range(1, N_ITEMS + 1):
        box_id = assignments[i].box_id
        if box_id > max_box_id:
            max_box_id = box_id
    return max_box_id

calculated_objective_value = calculate_objective(item_box_assignments)
objective = calculated_objective_value

# -- Constraints --


# --- Auxiliary Variables ---
# Leave empty, if not required.
# --- constraints ---
def fits_in_box(
    items: Annotated[list[Item], Len(8, 8)],
    assignments: Annotated[list[BoxAssignment], Len(8, 8)],
    box_width: int,
    box_height: int
):
    for i in range(1, N_ITEMS + 1):
        item : Item = items[i]
        assignment : BoxAssignment = assignments[i]
        assert assignment.x + item.width <= box_width
        assert assignment.y + item.height <= box_height

fits_in_box(ITEMS, item_box_assignments, BOX_WIDTH, BOX_HEIGHT)

# --- constraints ---

# --- objective ---
def calculate_objective(assignments: Annotated[list[int], Len(8, 8)]) -> int:
    max_box = 0
    for i in range(1, N_ITEMS + 1):
        box_nr = assignments[i]
        if box_nr > max_box:
            max_box = box_nr
    return max_box

def fits_in_box(items: Annotated[list[Item], Len(8, 8)], positions: Annotated[list[Position], Len(8, 8)], assignments: Annotated[list[int], Len(8, 8)]):
    for i in range(1, N_ITEMS + 1):
        item: Item = items[i]
        pos: Position = positions[i]
        assert pos.x + item.width <= BOX_WIDTH
        assert pos.y + item.height <= BOX_HEIGHT

fits_in_box(ITEMS, x_y_positions, item_box_assignments)

def no_overlap(items: Annotated[list[Item], Len(8, 8)], positions: Annotated[list[Position], Len(8, 8)], assignments: Annotated[list[int], Len(8, 8)]):
    for i in range(1, N_ITEMS + 1):
        for j in range(i + 1, N_ITEMS + 1):
            if assignments[i] == assignments[j]:
                pos_i: Position = positions[i]
                pos_j: Position = positions[j]
                item_i: Item = items[i]
                item_j: Item = items[j]
                assert (pos_i.x + item_i.width <= pos_j.x) or (pos_j.x + item_j.width <= pos_i.x) or (pos_i.y + item_i.height <= pos_j.y) or (pos_j.y + item_j.height <= pos_i.y)

```python
from typing import Annotated
from pydantic import Field

Item = DSRecord({
    "width": Annotated[int, Field(strict=True, ge=1, le=5)],
    "height": Annotated[int, Field(strict=True, ge=1, le=9)]
})

Position = DSRecord({
    "x": Annotated[int, Field(strict=True, ge=0, le=5)],
    "y": Annotated[int, Field(strict=True, ge=0, le=12)]
})
```



# --- Constants ---
BOX_HEIGHT : int = 12
BOX_WIDTH : int = 5
ITEM1 : Item = {"width": 3, "height": 4}
ITEM2 : Item = {"width": 1, "height": 2}
ITEM3 : Item = {"width": 5, "height": 4}
ITEM4 : Item = {"width": 2, "height": 4}
ITEM5 : Item = {"width": 1, "height": 3}
ITEM6 : Item = {"width": 5, "height": 9}
ITEM7 : Item = {"width": 5, "height": 3}
ITEM8 : Item = {"width": 5, "height": 1}
ITEMS : Annotated[list[Item], Len(8, 8)] = [ITEM1, ITEM2, ITEM3, ITEM4, ITEM5, ITEM6, ITEM7, ITEM8]
N_ITEMS : int = 8
nr_used_boxes : Annotated[int, Field(strict=True, ge=1, le=8)]

# -- Objective --


objective = nr_used_boxes

# --- objective ---
def calculate_objective(assignments: Annotated[list[int], Len(8, 8)]) -> int:
    max_box = 0
    for i in range(1, N_ITEMS + 1):
        box_nr = assignments[i]
        if box_nr > max_box:
            max_box = box_nr
    return max_box

calculated_objective_value = calculate_objective(item_box_assignments)
objective = calculated_objective_value

# --- constraints ---
def fits_in_box(items: Annotated[list[Item], Len(8, 8)], positions: Annotated[list[Position], Len(8, 8)], assignments: Annotated[list[int], Len(8, 8)]):
    for i in range(1, N_ITEMS + 1):
        item: Item = items[i]
        pos: Position = positions[i]
        assert pos.x + item.width <= BOX_WIDTH
        assert pos.y + item.height <= BOX_HEIGHT

fits_in_box(ITEMS, x_y_positions, item_box_assignments)

def no_overlap(items: Annotated[list[Item], Len(8, 8)], positions: Annotated[list[Position], Len(8, 8)], assignments: Annotated[list[int], Len(8, 8)]):
    for i in range(1, N_ITEMS + 1):
        for j in range(i + 1, N_ITEMS + 1):
            if assignments[i] == assignments[j]:
                pos_i: Position = positions[i]
                pos_j: Position = positions[j]
                item_i: Item = items[i]
                item_j: Item = items[j]
                assert (pos_i.x + item_i.width <= pos_j.x) or (pos_j.x + item_j.width <= pos_i.x) or (pos_i.y + item_i.height <= pos_j.y) or (pos_j.y + item_j.height <= pos_i.y)

no_overlap(ITEMS, x_y_positions, item_box_assignments)
